WC(1)                                    User Commands                                   WC(1)[m
[m
[1mNAME[0m[m
       wc - print newline, word, and byte counts for each file[m
[m
[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
       [1mwc[0m [[4mOPTION[24m]... [[4mFILE[24m]...[m
       [1mwc[0m [[4mOPTION[24m]... [4m--files0-from=F[24m[m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       Print  newline,  word, and byte counts for each FILE, and a total line if more than one[m
       FILE is specified.  A word is a non-zero-length sequence  of  characters  delimited  by[m
       white space.[m
[m
       With no FILE, or when FILE is -, read standard input.[m
[m
       The options below may be used to select which counts are printed, always in the follow-[m
       ing order: newline, word, character, byte, maximum line length.[m
[m
       [1m-c[0m, [1m--bytes[0m[m
              print the byte counts[m
[m
       [1m-m[0m, [1m--chars[0m[m
              print the character counts[m
[m
       [1m-l[0m, [1m--lines[0m[m
              print the newline counts[m
[m
       [1m--files0-from[0m=[4mF[24m[m
              read input from the files specified by NUL-terminated names in file F; If F is -[m
              then read names from standard input[m
[m
       [1m-L[0m, [1m--max-line-length[0m[m
              print the maximum display width[m
[7m Manual page wc(1) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[H[2J[H[H[2J[HWC(1)                                    User Commands                                   WC(1)[m

function L   (x,y) {if (gnuplot.pattern.length > 0) DL(x,y); else gnuplot.L(x,y);};
function Dot (x,y) {gnuplot.Dot(x/10.,y/10.);};
function Pt  (N,x,y,w) {gnuplot.Pt(N,x/10.,y/10.,w/10.);};
function R   (x,y,w,h) {gnuplot.R(x,y,w,h);};
function T   (x,y,fontsize,justify,string) {gnuplot.T(x,y,fontsize,justify,string);};
function TR  (x,y,angle,fontsize,justify,string) {gnuplot.TR(x,y,angle,fontsize,justify,string);};
function bp  (x,y) {gnuplot.bp(x,y);};
function cfp () {gnuplot.cfp();};
function cfsp() {gnuplot.cfsp();};

gnuplot.hypertext_list = [];
gnuplot.on_hypertext = -1;
function Hypertext(x,y,w,text) {
    newtext = {x:x, y:y, w:w, text:text};
    gnuplot.hypertext_list.push(newtext);
}
